[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA critical security issue was flagged by the Jazzer fuzzer harness: a file path [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal vulnerability. During an archive expansion operation, the sanitizer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected use of a path containing “..” segments that escape the intended output [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory, triggering a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue identification  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The Jazzer sanitizer `FilePathTraversal` raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception when the code attempted to expand an archive to a path including [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m”. The offending path was  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp9626160909472083664/output/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  File path traversal: untrusted input allows directory traversal via “..” [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegments, potentially escaping designated output directories.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Call chain and observations  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` invokes the expansion logic on [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer-supplied data.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The call stack proceeds through [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmultiple [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverloads/recursions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Before writing files, `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook` inspects the target[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. `FilePathTraversal.check` detects the traversal pattern and aborts with a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity exception.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important findings  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in the path sanitizer, not the harness; it flags [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially dangerous file extraction.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The Expander example code allows paths containing “..” to be passed to [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile-creation routines before sanitization.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The JAZZER sanitizer hook is triggered on the first argument to the file write [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The `Expander.expand` methods in [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`: how file paths are [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalized and passed.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`pathFirstArgHook`, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`checkPath`, `check`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any code that resolves or constructs file system paths for extraction [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Interaction between the fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the Expander [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary API.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis analysis covers the detection of a file path traversal vulnerability during [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz testing, highlights the relevant stack frames, and identifies code regions for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma more comprehensive review.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The fuzzer triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception from Jazzer’s        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         file-path-traversal sanitizer when running the `ExpanderFuzzer`, indicating a       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         potential “zip-slip” directory traversal in `Expander.expand`. A patch was applied  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to `Expander.java` to replace the old `targetPath` resolution with a normalized     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `targetEntryPath`, add a pre–write check against escaping the target directory, and [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         adjust directory-creation calls. After applying the patch, the codebase failed to   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         compile: references to the now-removed `targetPath` variable remained in several    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         spots, leading the Java compiler to report “cannot find symbol: variable            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         targetPath” in `Expander.java`.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - A Jazzer sanitizer [1m([0m`FilePathTraversal`[1m)[0m detected a file-path traversal when      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Expander.expand` processed an archive entry.                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The stack trace shows the exception originating from                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`, invoked by `Expander.expand`, and propagated  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         up through `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The sanitizer reports that an entry resolves outside the intended extraction      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory [1m([0me.g., via `“..[35m/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m”` sequences[1m)[0m.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Important Observations                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The failure is triggered by invalid or malicious archive entries whose normalized [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         paths escape the target directory.                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The sanitizer halts execution by throwing `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`, marking  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         this as a security-sensitive issue.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The root of the problem lies in how `Expander` currently resolves entry paths     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0musing `[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mtargetDirPath[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m without an explicit traversal check.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - In `Expander.java`, the patch removes the old `targetPath` declaration and        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         instead declares:                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```java                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           final Path targetEntryPath = nullTarget                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               ? null                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               : [1;35mtargetDirPath.resolve[0m[1m([0m[1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - It then checks:                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```java                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           if [1m([0m!nullTarget && ![1;35mtargetEntryPath.startsWith[0m[1m([0mtargetDirPath[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               throw new [1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0m[32m"Zip slip detected: entry "[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                   + [1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m + [32m" resolves outside target: "[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                   + targetEntryPath[1m)[0m;                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Directory-creation logic was updated to use `targetEntryPath` instead of          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `targetPath`.                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - However, the patch left references such as:                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```java                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           final Path parent = nullTarget ? null : [1;35mtargetPath.getParent[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           which refer to the now-deleted `targetPath`.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Build Log After Patch                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Maven recompilation of `org.apache.commons.compress:commons-compress` fails with: [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           Expander.java:[1m[[0m[1;36m92[0m,[1;36m76[0m[1m][0m cannot find symbol                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             symbol: variable targetPath                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             location: class Expander                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The compiler error pinpoints an unresolved identifier at the amended expansion    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         loop [1m([0maround lines [1;36m90[0m–[1;36m100[0m of `Expander.java`[1m)[0m.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Areas for Further Investigation                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The code around `Expander.expand`, specifically the loop that resolves and writes [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entries, to ensure all uses of the old `targetPath` are replaced with the new       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `targetEntryPath`.                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Any auxiliary methods or overloads [1m([0me.g., `resolveIn`, directory-creation         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         helpers[1m)[0m for consistency in path normalization and traversal checks.                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Related archiver and compressor example classes to see if similar path-resolution [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         patterns exist elsewhere.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The interaction between `[1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`, normalization, and `resolve` to    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         validate that no edge cases remain unhandled.                                       [2m                [0m
